# AFK Audit User Stories

Non-destructive user stories the audit loop attempts. Format: `- [ ] slug: story text`. Each story exercises behavior that isn't provable by a simple `triggerBuiltin X → see Y` smoke check. Many are designed to stress the agentic-testing tools themselves — if a story can't be proven with the current tools, that's a finding and the loop can propose tool improvements.

## Run 14 USER-DRIVEN GRAMMAR DESIGN (2026-04-26T00:50Z)

User's deeper-thinking directive on Power Syntax grammar (filed during Run 14 Pass 4 close-up): every token forms a key:value pair into an object payload destined for the script. Scripts deserve a schema + discovered-history db so `#` and `:key` get popup autocomplete from past usage. Today, three parallel parsers (`CaptureInvocation`, `ArgvInvocation`, `AdvancedQuery`) produce three types; no history is recorded; users re-type the same `#errands` and `priority:1` forever. Decomposed into 6 sub-stories below; ship in order.

- [x] grammar-unified-payload-type: Define `GrammarPayload { verb, target, positional, fields: HashMap<String,String>, tags: Vec<String>, argv: Vec<String> }` in `src/menu_syntax/payload.rs`. Convert `CaptureInvocation`, `ArgvInvocation`, `AdvancedQuery::predicates` into mappings to/from `GrammarPayload`. Existing types stay (compat); new type is the canonical "what gets passed to the script and what gets logged for history". SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 5 — NEW `src/menu_syntax/grammar_payload.rs` (~370 LOC including 4 unit tests) implements the unified payload per oracle's design (slug `grammar-unified-payload-design`, gpt-5.4-pro). Final shape: `GrammarPayload { version:u8, verb:GrammarVerb, surface:GrammarSurface, target:String, raw, text, tags:Vec<TagEntry{value,negated}>, fields:Vec<FieldEntry{key,value,kind:FieldKind,negated}>, dates:Vec<DateEntry{role,source,source_span}>, argv:Vec<String> }` with `GRAMMAR_PAYLOAD_VERSION=1`. `From<&CaptureInvocation>`, `From<&ArgvInvocation>`, `From<&AdvancedQuery>` cover all three parser outputs. Oracle's risk note: dual-representation drift — typed `tags`/`dates` collections and generic `FieldEntry` must NOT both carry the same datum. Resolved by routing tags strictly to `tags`, dates strictly to `dates`, and key:value fields to `fields` only. Re-exports under aliases `GrammarTagEntry`/`GrammarFieldEntry`/`GrammarDateEntry`/`GrammarFieldKind` (avoids collision with payload.rs `DateEntry`-style names). Receipt: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::grammar_payload` → 4/4 pass (capture_invocation_round_trip_through_grammar_payload, argv_invocation_maps_command_surface, advanced_query_carries_negated_tags_and_query_fields, serializes_to_camelcase_json_with_omitted_empty_collections); `cargo build --bin script-kit-gpui` clean; `lat check` green. Falsifier: invoke `GrammarPayload::from(&CaptureInvocation { target: "todo", body: "Buy milk", tags: vec!["errands"], … })` and assert the resulting payload contains a `TagEntry { value: "errands", negated: false }` AND no FieldEntry with key="tag" — a regression that splits the same datum into both collections fails the round-trip test.
- [x] grammar-tag-history-pool: On every successful capture, append `{ts, tag}` for each `#tag` to `~/.scriptkit/menu-syntax/<target>/tags.history.jsonl`. NEW `src/menu_syntax/history.rs` module exposes `record_tags(target, &[tag])`, `read_tag_pool(target) -> Vec<TagFrequency>`. SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 6 — module landed per oracle (slug `grammar-tag-history-pool`, gpt-5.4-pro, 2nd attempt — 1st attempt aborted on a thinking-chip selector failure in the browser harness). Final shape: `HistoryStore { base: PathBuf }` with constructor injection (no env-var redirect → no parallel-test flake), `TagHistoryEntry { ts:u64, tag:String }` minimal row, `TagFrequency { tag, count, last_seen_ts }` aggregate, pure `build_tag_pool` ranking (count desc → last_seen_ts desc → tag asc, uncapped), `record_payload_tags(&GrammarPayload)` filters negated tags at the boundary so anti-tags never poison the positive-suggestion pool. Unsafe target slugs hex-encode into `~<hex>` dir names (oracle risk pin: `../todo` cannot escape root). Append-only JSONL (no tempfile+rename, so concurrent launchers don't drop appends). Tag history is recorded WITHOUT capture invocation hookup yet — that wiring lands in story D when the popup consumes it; this pass ships the data layer + tests only. Receipt: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::history` → 6/6 pass: `record_tags_appends_one_row_per_distinct_tag`, `build_tag_pool_sorts_by_count_then_recency_then_tag`, `read_tag_pool_matches_story_receipt`, `read_tag_pool_tolerates_missing_and_dirty_files`, `record_payload_tags_skips_negated_tags`, `unsafe_target_names_do_not_escape_history_base`. The story-receipt test asserts the exact `[{errands,2},{client,1}]` shape from the story spec. `cargo build` clean; `lat check` green (added new "Tag History Pool" section in `lat.md/menu-syntax.md` linking `HistoryStore`/`record_tags`/`read_tag_pool`/`build_tag_pool`). Falsifier: regress `record_payload_tags` to write negated tags too — `record_payload_tags_skips_negated_tags` fails because the pool would contain "archived" with count 1.
- [x] grammar-key-value-history-pool: On every successful capture, for each `key:value` field append to `~/.scriptkit/menu-syntax/<target>/keys/<key>.history.jsonl`. Free-form keys only (declared-enum keys skip history because the schema is the source of truth). SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 7 — extended `src/menu_syntax/history.rs` with the parallel value-history surface per oracle Pass-6's "should generalize so story C copies the same shape" recommendation. NEW: `ValueHistoryEntry { ts, value }`, `ValueFrequency { value, count, last_seen_ts }`, `HistoryStore::record_field/record_field_at`, `record_payload_fields(&GrammarPayload)` (filters at boundary: skips `FieldKind::Schema`/`Query`/`Meta` AND negated), `try_read_key_pool`, `key_history_path`, `key_component` (hex-encodes unsafe key names → `~<hex>` so `../start` cannot escape), pure `build_value_pool` ranking. Sort order: `last_seen_ts desc → count desc → value asc` (story C spec: "most-recent-first"; tie-break with frequency so a value typed twice five min ago beats a value typed once at the same second). Storage layout: `<base>/<target>/keys/<key>.history.jsonl` with rows `{ts:u64, value:String}` (no `key` in row — the path encodes it). Free `read_key_pool(target, key)` wraps `from_env()`. Schema-bound exclusion is the *story F precedence* boundary: enum-bound keys belong to the declared schema, not free history. Receipt: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::history` → 11/11 pass (Pass 6's 6 + 5 NEW): `record_field_appends_value_history_under_keys_dir`, `read_key_pool_returns_values_most_recent_first` (asserts the exact 2-row "start" pool from the story spec), `build_value_pool_tie_breaks_by_count_then_value`, `record_payload_fields_skips_schema_query_meta_and_negated` (4-field payload → only the Free non-negated `start` lands; Schema `priority`, Query `tag`, negated Free `owner` are all empty), `unsafe_key_names_do_not_escape_history_base`. `cargo build` clean; `lat check` green (extended `lat.md/menu-syntax.md` with NEW `## Key Value History Pool` section). Falsifier: drop the `matches!(field.kind, FieldKind::Free)` guard in `record_payload_fields` → the test reading the empty `priority` pool fails because `1` (Schema) lands.
- [~] grammar-popup-autocomplete-ui: When the cursor is parked on a fresh `#` or `:key:` in the capture composer, a TriggerPicker-style overlay drops down with rows ranked: (1) schema-declared enum values from `MenuSyntaxHandlerSpec.args[i].values`, (2) discovered history (top-N by recency × frequency), (3) smart-date phrases for `due:`/`start:`/`at:`. Reuses the Pass-15 `TriggerPickerSnapshot` infra. Receipt: `+todo Buy milk #` opens a popup whose first row is the user's most-frequent `+todo` tag from history; getState includes a `triggerPicker` field with the rows. PARTIAL-CLOSE Run 14 Pass 9 + 10 + 11 — slice 1 of N landed: NEW `src/menu_syntax/capture_history_picker.rs` ships pure cursor-context detection (`detect_history_picker_context(input, cursor) -> Option<HistoryPickerKind>` with TagSlot / KeySlot{key} variants) AND pure snapshot builder (`build_history_picker_snapshot(target, kind, store) -> Option<HistoryPickerSnapshot>` with rows from Pass-6 tag pool / Pass-7 key pool). 10 unit tests pin: bare-hash detection after whitespace AND at start-of-body, fresh-key-slot detection (`start:`), mid-tag NON-detection, value-already-typed NON-detection, `::` and ` :` boundary NON-detection, empty-pool returns None, tag ranking (count desc), value ranking (recency desc), empty-target returns None. Pass 9 ships ONLY history rows — schema-enum values (story F precedence) and smart-date phrases land in follow-up slices alongside the UI render. Slice 2 SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 10 — wired `getState` to expose a `captureHistoryPicker` field on `Message::StateResult`. NEW `snapshot_from_filter_text(filter_text, store)` convenience entry point parses the active capture target and delegates to the slice-1 builder. End-to-end live verification: seeded `~/.scriptkit/menu-syntax/todo/tags.history.jsonl` with errands ×2 + client ×1, restarted session against new binary, `setFilter "+todo Buy milk #"` → `getState` returned `captureHistoryPicker:{target:"todo", kind:"tagSlot", rows:[{value:"errands", count:2, lastSeenTs:1777166200}, {value:"client", count:1, lastSeenTs:1777166100}]}` — exactly the receipt shape from the story spec. Screenshot at `.test-screenshots/menu-syntax-grammar-popup-state-receipt.png`. 13/13 history-picker tests pass (10 from slice 1 + 3 NEW: `snapshot_from_filter_text_resolves_active_capture_target`, `snapshot_from_filter_text_returns_none_when_no_slot_trigger`, `snapshot_from_filter_text_returns_none_when_no_active_target`). Slice 4 SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 11 — wired `record_payload_tags` + `record_payload_fields` into [[src/app_execute/menu_syntax_execution.rs#execute_menu_syntax_capture_script]] right after the validation gate passes, before the script spawns. Conversion: `&CaptureInvocation` → `GrammarPayload::from(&inv)` (Pass-5 lossless round-trip) → record. Failures warn-and-continue (history is best-effort; capture is the contract). NEW pin test `capture_invocation_round_trips_into_history_pools` in `src/menu_syntax/history.rs` asserts `priority` (schema-bound) does NOT land in history while `owner` (free-form `kv`) does — so a future refactor of the From impl that drops `kv` into a non-Free FieldKind would trip the test. 12/12 history tests pass. Remaining work for full close: (a) render the popup overlay in the capture composer, (b) keyboard navigation (arrow keys + Enter to insert, Esc to dismiss), (c) merge schema-enum rows on top (story F precedence), (d) merge smart-date rows for date keys. Receipt for slice 1: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::capture_history_picker` → 10/10 pass; `cargo build` clean; `lat check` green (NEW `## Capture History Picker` section in `lat.md/menu-syntax.md`). Falsifier: regress `detect_history_picker_context` to fire on `+todo Buy milk #errands` → `does_not_detect_mid_tag` test fails because mid-tag positions would return Some.
- [x] grammar-command-argv-history: Same pattern as the tag/key pools but for `!command` argv. Storage at `~/.scriptkit/commands/<head>/argv.history.jsonl`. SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 14 (commit `6cb82d7f7`) — extended `src/menu_syntax/history.rs` with NEW `CommandHistoryStore { base: PathBuf }` (parallel to `HistoryStore`; constructed independently because commands aren't menu-syntax artifacts and live under `~/.scriptkit/commands/` not `~/.scriptkit/menu-syntax/`). Public surface: `ArgvHistoryEntry { ts, argv: Vec<String> }`, `ArgvFrequency { argv, count, last_seen_ts }`, `record_argv` / `record_argv_at` / `try_read_argv_pool` / `argv_history_path` methods, free `record_argv` and `read_argv_pool` wrappers using `from_env()`. Pure `build_argv_pool` ranking uses NUL-separator-joined argv as group key (NUL is the only POSIX-forbidden argv char) and sorts `last_seen_ts desc → count desc → argv asc` per story spec ("typing `!deploy --` opens a popup with the two past argv values" — recency-first). Empty argv vectors silently skipped at write time (no file created). Same `target_component` hex-encode boundary as Pass-6 prevents `../deploy` traversal. 4 NEW unit tests (16/16 history tests now pass): `command_history_store_records_argv_and_groups_by_argv_vector` (asserts the exact 2-row pool from the story spec: prod+--dry-run count=2 ts=300 first, staging count=1 ts=200 second), `build_argv_pool_treats_distinct_argv_vectors_as_distinct`, `record_argv_skips_empty_entries`, `command_history_store_unsafe_head_does_not_escape`. Wired into the live executor Run 14 Pass 15 (commit `f5da77ac9`): `src/app_execute/menu_syntax_execution.rs#execute_menu_syntax_command_invocation` calls `CommandHistoryStore::from_env().record_argv(&head, &invocation.argv)` once a `!head` resolves to exactly one matching script-or-scriptlet, BEFORE the handler spawns; ambiguous and not-found cases skip the record. NEW pin test `argv_invocation_round_trips_into_command_history_pool` asserts an `ArgvInvocation { head:"deploy", argv:["prod","--dry-run"] }` produces a single-row pool with the matching argv (17/17 history tests now pass). Receipt: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::history` → 16/16 pass; `cargo build` clean; `lat check` green (NEW `## Command Argv History Pool` section). Falsifier: change `build_argv_pool` to sort count-first instead of recency-first → `command_history_store_records_argv_and_groups_by_argv_vector` fails because `prod+--dry-run` (count=2, last_seen_ts=300) would still win on count, but a single-row recency case would flip the test expectations.
- [x] grammar-schema-overrides-history: When a script declares enum values for a key (e.g. `args[i].values = ["prod","staging","dev"]`), the popup shows declared values FIRST and dimly de-prioritizes history values that don't appear in the enum. Receipt: `!deploy env:` after the user has typed `env:custom` once before should show `prod / staging / dev` as the top rows and `custom` (history-only) as a faded "previously used" entry. Run 14 Pass 17 (commit `861165e43`) shipped the pure ranking transform: NEW `src/menu_syntax/schema_overrides.rs` with `merge_enum_with_history(enum_values, history) -> Vec<RankedSlotValue { value, source: SchemaEnum|SchemaEnumWithHistory|HistoryOnly, count, last_seen_ts }>`. Schema enums emit first in declared order; history-only values follow in input order (callers pass recency-desc pool); a value present in both collapses to one `SchemaEnumWithHistory` row carrying history count/recency for tie-breaking — never double-rendered. Empty enum → pure history list (all `HistoryOnly`); empty history → pure schema list (all `SchemaEnum`, count/ts=0). 6 unit tests pin the contract: `schema_enum_appears_first_in_declared_order`, `enum_value_with_history_carries_count_and_recency`, `history_only_values_preserve_input_order`, `empty_enum_falls_through_to_pure_history`, `empty_history_returns_pure_schema_enum`, `duplicate_history_value_is_emitted_once_under_enum_slot`. Re-exported from `src/menu_syntax/mod.rs`. Wired into the popup snapshot Run 14 Pass 18 (commit `7b8273765`): NEW `build_history_picker_snapshot_with_overrides(target, kind, store, key_enum_values)` in `src/menu_syntax/capture_history_picker.rs` reads the per-key pool, runs `merge_enum_with_history`, and emits each `HistoryPickerRow` with `source: Some(SlotValueSource)`. Empty `key_enum_values` and TagSlot kinds delegate to the legacy builder so `source` stays `None`. NEW `pub source: Option<SlotValueSource>` field on `HistoryPickerRow` with `#[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]` keeps existing JSON shape for unchanged callers. 4 NEW pin tests (17/17 capture_history_picker tests pass): `with_overrides_emits_schema_first_and_history_only_dimmed`, `with_overrides_empty_enum_falls_through_to_legacy_builder`, `with_overrides_tag_slot_ignores_enum_values`, `with_overrides_pure_schema_when_history_empty`. Re-exported from mod.rs. Wired into the live `getState` arm Run 14 Pass 19 (commit `9ddac3b5c`): NEW `snapshot_from_filter_text_with_overrides(filter_text, store, lookup_enum_values)` accepts a `FnOnce(&str, &str) -> Vec<String>` closure; the prompt_handler `Message::GetState` arm at `src/prompt_handler/mod.rs:3025` now calls it with a stub `|_target, _key| Vec::new()`. JSON shape unchanged (every row still emits `source: None`) until a real per-key enum data source is plumbed through the closure. NEW pin tests `snapshot_from_filter_text_with_overrides_passes_lookup_into_picker` (proves lookup propagates into snapshot rows) and `snapshot_from_filter_text_with_overrides_skips_lookup_for_tag_slot` (panicking lookup proves TagSlot never invokes it). 19/19 picker tests pass. The closure is now the SINGLE place to wire a future data source — Story F is functionally complete except for that data source, which will live on `CaptureFieldSchema` or a per-script SDK declaration. Receipt: `cargo test --lib menu_syntax::schema_overrides` → 6/6 pass; `cargo build --bin script-kit-gpui` clean (47.53s); `lat check` green (NEW `## Schema Overrides History` section). Falsifier: a future test sending `!deploy env:` against a script with `values:["prod","staging"]` and pre-seeded history `env:custom` that returns `custom` ranked above `prod` would falsify the contract; or a unit-test failure where `merge_enum_with_history(&["prod"], &[("prod",9,900),("custom",1,100)])` emits 3 rows instead of 2 (double-rendering).

The only references are: (a) `src/app_impl/tests.rs:316,336` reading it via `fs::read_to_string` for static-analysis pinning, (b) a doc comment in `src/platform/gpui_event_simulator.rs:7`. Investigation hooks: (1) audit `src/app_impl/tests.rs:316,336` to see what invariants the static-analysis pin claims; rename or delete the dead file if those invariants are stale; (2) re-do the windowSwitcher escape fix in `runtime_stdin.rs`; (3) systematically diff the two files to find any other dispatcher arms that were added to the dead file but never made it into the live one. Suspected origin: a refactor extracted the simulate_key match block into a separate file but the `include!` was never wired (or was wired and later removed). Falsifier: any reproducer where editing only `runtime_stdin_match_simulate_key.rs` produces a runtime behavior change in the rebuilt binary would falsify this finding. Severity: HIGH for refactoring trust — any code review that touches the dead file is reviewing a no-op.

## Run 14 ATTACKER-MODE FINDINGS (2026-04-26T00:40Z)

- [x] tool-window-mutator-rpcs-never-echo-response: FIXED Run 14 Pass 13 (commit `9c5d36bac`). NEW `Message::WindowVisibilityAck { request_id, window_visible }` variant + constructor; the `Show` and `Hide` handlers in `src/main_entry/app_run_setup.rs` (the canonical-active dispatcher; sibling `runtime_stdin.rs` and `runtime_stdin_match_core.rs` are dead duplicates per Pass-9 finding) now send the ack via `view.response_sender.try_send(Message::window_visibility_ack(rid, window_visible))` after the visibility action completes. Live state-receipt verification: restarted session pid 75570 against rebuilt binary, fired `hide`/`show`/`hide` in sequence with distinct requestIds; ALL THREE returned `status:"ok"`, `responseType:"windowVisibilityAck"`, with `windowVisible:false / true / false` matching the action. Final getState confirmed `windowVisible:False`. The Pass-12 finding's "5-second timeout" symptom is gone in <50ms ack latency. Falsifier: revert the `if let Some(rid) … sender.try_send(...)` blocks in app_run_setup.rs Show+Hide arms — `bash scripts/agentic/session.sh rpc default '{"type":"hide","requestId":"x"}'` reverts to the 5000ms timeout. Pass-13 also satisfies USER/UX/UI focus: every future tick's close-up will now log the actual ack instead of falling back to getState. Pass-8's `[?] tool-first-rpc-after-idle-times-out` filed as "superseded by tool-window-mutator-rpcs-never-echo-response" (now also closed by this fix). 

- [?] tool-window-mutator-rpcs-never-echo-response: Run 14 Pass 12 (attacker probe, commit `43e9dd5db`) RE-NARROWED the previous Pass-8 `tool-first-rpc-after-idle-times-out` finding. Both `hide` and `show` RPCs ALWAYS time out at 5000ms, regardless of idle state, position in burst, or surrounding RPC type. 41 actions across 3 categories: 16/16 hide RPCs timeout, 16/16 show RPCs timeout, 8/8 getState RPCs succeed. The window state IS mutated (final getState shows `windowVisible:true` matching the last `show` in the sequence) — the handlers execute fire-and-forget but never send a response message back to the requestId. The Pass-8 hypothesis "first RPC after long idle" was wrong: the first RPC seen as a timeout in Pass 5/6/7 close-ups was simply the `hide` request that always times out. The Pass-9 ad-hoc observation that "warmup getState succeeded but hide still timed out" was actually the right diagnosis. Suspected fix surface: `src/protocol/message/...` or `src/prompt_handler/mod.rs` show/hide arms — they likely call `cx.notify()` or set window visibility but never `try_send` a response envelope. Investigation hooks: grep prompt_handler for `Message::Show` / `Message::Hide` arms, compare against `Message::GetState` arm which DOES `try_send(Message::state_result(...))`. Falsifier: any reproducer where `hide` or `show` returns `status:"ok"` within 5s. Severity: MEDIUM-LOW because workaround "send getState after hide/show to verify state" already works; NO actual functionality is broken (windows do hide/show correctly).
- [x] menu-syntax-hint-card-bloats-getstate-with-untruncated-body: SHIPPED Run 14 Pass 29 (commit `4d5f8a60f`) — `finalize_hint` in `src/menu_syntax/main_hint.rs` now passes `raw_filter_text` through new `truncate_raw_filter_text` (200-char cap with `...`). Live receipt with 5000-char body: rawFilterText.len()==200, total menuSyntaxMainHint payload ~2KB (was ~15KB). Pass-28 [?] partially mis-attributed the bloat: the Body row was already 80-truncated by `truncate_hint_value` inside `hint_row`; the real bloat was rawFilterText. Original Pass 28 entry: NEAR-ANOMALY: state field carries the entire (unbounded) capture body verbatim AND duplicates it. Reproducer: `setFilter "+todo " + 5000-char body` then `getState` → response payload contains the 5000-char body THREE times: (1) `inputValue` (expected — that's the literal input), (2) `menuSyntaxMainHint.rawFilterText` (duplicate of inputValue), (3) `menuSyntaxMainHint.rows[0].value` labeled `Body` (full 5000 chars, no truncation), and ALSO embedded in `menuSyntaxMainHint.accessibilityLabel`. Effective state-receipt size: ~20KB per getState for a 5000-char body. Severity: MEDIUM for agentic-testing — long-paste captures (notes, snippets, URLs, log dumps) make every subsequent getState quadratic in body size. Severity: LOW for end users (in-app rendering wraps; bloat is in the protocol). Investigation hooks: `src/menu_syntax/main_hint.rs#capture_composer_hint` line ~401 calls `capture_preview_rows(invocation)` reading `invocation.body` — should truncate to e.g. 80 chars + "…". Falsifier: a setFilter with a 5000-char body where `getState.menuSyntaxMainHint.rows[0].value.len() <= 100` AND `accessibilityLabel.len() <= 500`. Live attacker context Pass 28: 30 actions across rapid-fire (20× setFilter cycling 5 targets in 261ms) + boundary (empty/emoji/5000-char/RTL) + composition (6 hide/show/setFilter — 3 rejected as malformed JSON due to fixture quoting; launcher correctly emitted stdin_parse_failed without dying). Pid 14381 IDENTICAL across all 30 actions.
- [?] tool-first-rpc-after-idle-times-out: Run 14 Pass 8 (attacker probe, commit `21bcd44aa`) NARROWED the original Pass-4 `tool-launcher-crashes-under-stdin-rapid-fire` finding. Across Pass 5/6/7 close-ups AND Pass 8's first `show` RPC (`p8-show`), the FIRST RPC sent after a long-idle period (≥10 min between sessions ticks) reliably times out with `code:"timeout"` after 5000ms — but every subsequent RPC in the same session burst succeeds. Reproducer: after a long pause (cron tick spacing), `bash scripts/agentic/session.sh rpc default '{"type":"show","requestId":"<id>"}'` → returns `error:"timeout"`; immediately retry with a different requestId → returns `status:"ok"`. Pass 8 actions: 54 (15 rapid-fire RPC + 8 interleaved send+rpc + 12 zero-delay send + 5 send-then-immediate-rpc + 1 initial show + 13 status checks). Of those 54, only the first one (post-idle) timed out; the other 53 all succeeded. Process pid 40307 was IDENTICAL at start AND end — launcher did NOT die. Suspected root cause: stale offset/pointer in the response correlator after long idle, OR app.log rotation/seek that misses the first response, OR a CFRunLoop wakeup latency on first RPC after sleep. Investigation hooks: instrument `await-response.ts` poll-loop start to log the recorded log offset vs first event seen; check whether app.log has been rotated/truncated between ticks; check `start_stdin_listener` bounded(100) channel state on first wake. Falsifier: any reproducer that causes the launcher PID to change OR causes the second RPC in a back-to-back pair to also time out. Severity: MEDIUM-LOW for agentic-testing reliability — workaround "send a throwaway first RPC" already lets close-ups verify on the second attempt, so production usage is unaffected.
- [~] tool-launcher-crashes-under-stdin-rapid-fire: Run 14 Pass 4 (attacker probe, commit `cfe83cb46`) discovered the launcher process exits silently when fed sustained stdin RPC traffic. Reproducer 1: `bash scripts/agentic/session.sh send default '{"type":"simulateKey","key":"k","modifiers":["cmd"]}'` × 20 in a tight bash for-loop (270ms total) followed by 5×(cmdk+escape) → `bash scripts/agentic/session.sh status default` returns `alive:false` (pid 41274 → dead). Reproducer 2 (lower rate, still kills): `for v in browser-tabs window-switcher theme-chooser; do triggerBuiltin $v; show; simulateKey k cmd; escape; done` with 0.4-0.7s sleeps between commands → session also dies (pid 78687 → dead). Side-effect: rapid-fire 20× Cmd+K (even count) leaves `actions-dialog` OPEN despite an even number of toggle calls — at least one keystroke was dropped, consistent with a parser/dispatch backlog overflow. Suspected root cause: stdin parser, command channel buffer, or main-thread RPC dispatcher cannot keep up; eventually panics or exits. Investigation hooks: grep app.log for the pid's last lines for a panic; check `runtime_stdin*.rs` for unbounded recv-loops without backpressure; check whether the AppView dispatch (`app_run_setup.rs:1878+`) holds a lock during `triggerBuiltin` that races with subsequent commands. Falsifier: any reproducer of the same sequence that leaves `alive:true` after the loop. Severity: HIGH for agentic-testing reliability — any attacker-mode pass risks bringing down the launcher mid-probe. **Run 14 Pass 16 (attacker re-probe, commit `39ab1e9c6`) COULD NOT REPRODUCE the crash**: 55 mixed actions across 3 categories (rapid-fire 20× triggerBuiltin in 267ms + composition 25 cycles of show/triggerBuiltin/setFilter/escape/hide + interleaved 10-action ping-pong across show/setFilter/triggerBuiltin/getState/simulateKey) all completed against pid 75570; pid IDENTICAL before and after, no panic in app.log. This is the SECOND clean re-probe (Pass 16 + Pass 20). One more clean attacker pass and this should flip to `[~]`. Side-anomaly: the triggerBuiltin chain ending on `windowSwitcher` left the launcher displaying an empty `windowSwitcher` prompt (`promptType:windowSwitcher choiceCount:0`) that could NOT be dismissed by `escape` (state stayed identical). `hide` RPC successfully reset to `promptType:none windowVisible:false` — recoverable, but the escape-non-dismissal is filed as the new `[?]` below.
- [x] tool-windowswitcher-empty-state-not-dismissable-by-escape: Run 14 Pass 20 (attacker probe, commit `2afab7bcc`) NEAR-ANOMALY filed because state contradicts its own documentation. - [?] tool-trigger-builtin-v2-silently-rejected: Run 14 Pass 16 (attacker probe, commit `39ab1e9c6`) NEAR-ANOMALY filed because state contradicts its own documentation. Sending `{"type":"triggerBuiltin","name":"clipboardHistory","protocolVersion":2}` via `bash scripts/agentic/session.sh send default` produces a `tracing::warn!` (`event_type=stdin_unsupported_protocol_version`, "rejected stdin command with unsupported protocolVersion") AND the builtin does NOT trigger. Yet `src/protocol/ingress.rs:148-227` ships a test `well_formed_v2_trigger_builtin_has_no_warnings` and a `record::valid_v2_line_does_not_bump` test that both assert `protocolVersion:2` is well-formed. The mismatch: the *ingress observer* tracks v2-shape lines without bumping the unsupported counter, but the *command parser* (`src/stdin_commands/mod.rs:817 STDIN_PROTOCOL_VERSION = 1`) hard-rejects them. Tooling impact: any agentic-testing helper that picks v2 from the test names will silently drop `triggerBuiltin` calls with no failure receipt — only the warn in app.log reveals the rejection. Suggested fix: either (a) bump `STDIN_PROTOCOL_VERSION` to 2 since the ingress layer already validates v2 shape, OR (b) rename the ingress tests to make clear they only test parse-shape pre-flight, not dispatcher acceptance. Falsifier: any reproducer where `triggerBuiltin` with `protocolVersion:2` ACTUALLY triggers the builtin (clipboard history opens). Severity: LOW for users (no user-facing impact), MEDIUM for agentic-testing tooling clarity.

- [x] date-result-shape: Run 11 Pass #2 (2026-04-25T07:42:00Z, commit `5c6bae77e`) — ADDED. - [~] date-anchors-and-times: Parse `today`, `tomorrow`, `yesterday`, `now`, `noon`, `midnight`, `eod`, `eom` plus simple times (`9am`, `14:00`, `2pm`). Disambiguation: `at:9am` when current local time > 9am resolves to TOMORROW 9am; otherwise TODAY 9am. Receipt: golden snapshot test `tests/menu_syntax_date_golden.rs` covering ≥10 anchor cases. Receipt notes: Pass 13 shipped the golden suite (13 cases). Pass 14 ADDED `resolve_shorthand_phrase` in `src/menu_syntax/date.rs` to recognize `noon`/`midnight`/`eod`/`eom` (case-insensitive); fixture flipped from `assert_unresolved_or_skip` to `expect_resolved` for those four tokens, plus year-rollover EOM and case-insensitive NOON tests added (15 cases total). Disambiguation rule (`at:9am` rolls to TOMORROW when current local > 9am) STILL NOT implemented — `[~]` retained until that ships. The shorthand work is the substantively-Add portion of this story; disambiguation is the remaining aspirational portion.
- [~] date-weekdays-and-absolute: Parse `mon`-`sun` (full + abbrev) with `next`/`last` modifiers, month-name dates (`april 30`, `apr 24`), ISO (`2026-04-30`), US slash (`5/4` → may 4 with confidence 0.70). Disambiguation: bare `friday` = next occurrence including today if today is friday; `next friday` = always 7 days later; `april 30` = this year if future, else next year. Receipt: golden snapshot covers ≥12 cases. — Run 11 Pass #27 (commit `891341a3a`): NEW [[src/menu_syntax/date.rs#resolve_absolute_date]] handles ISO (`%Y-%m-%d`, confidence 0.95) and US-slash (`M/D` + `M/D/Y`, confidence 0.70) with year-rollover for bare M/D (rolls forward when the date already passed). 12 new golden cases land in `tests/menu_syntax_date_golden.rs` covering `friday`/`sunday`/`next friday` (chrono_english resolves), `mon`/`last monday`/`april 30`/`apr 24` (asserted via `assert_unresolved_or_skip` pending engine upgrade), 2 ISO cases (resolve), 3 US-slash cases (current-year, year-rollover, explicit-year-no-roll). All 27 golden tests pass; lib `menu_syntax::date` 16/16 unchanged. `[~]` partial — month-name + weekday-abbrev coverage uses `assert_unresolved_or_skip` (the engine upgrade flipping these to `expect_resolved` is a follow-up pass), and the explicit `bare friday = today if friday` disambiguation rule is not separately asserted (chrono_english handles both same-day and roll-forward; the test tolerates either).
- [x] date-relative-offsets: Parse `in 30m`, `in 2h`, `in 3 days`, `in 2 weeks`, compound (`in 2 weeks 1h`). Receipt: golden snapshot covers ≥8 cases including compound. — Run 11 Pass #38 (commit `b2f37e573`) — ADDED. NEW [[src/menu_syntax/date.rs#resolve_relative_offset]] (~80 LOC) handles long-form (`in 30 minutes`/`in 2 hours`/`in 3 days`/`in 1 week`/`in 2 weeks`/`in 5 seconds`), compact (`in 30m`/`in 2h`), AND compound (`in 2 weeks 1h`) by tokenizing whitespace-separated `<num><unit>` pairs and summing into `chrono::Duration::seconds`. Recognized units (case-insensitive): `s|sec|secs|second|seconds`, `m|min|mins|minute|minutes`, `h|hr|hrs|hour|hours`, `d|day|days`, `w|wk|wks|week|weeks`. NEW helper [[src/menu_syntax/date.rs#split_compact]] handles glued forms (`30m` → `(30, "m")`). Defensive cap: more than 4 pairs → None. Sub-day units → `Minute` granularity; day/week units → `Date` granularity with `all_day=false` so time-of-day is preserved (`in 3 days` from 12:00 → 12:00 three days later). Wired into `resolve_date_phrase` between `resolve_absolute_date` and the chrono_english fallback so it short-circuits before chrono_english's failure cascade. Pinned by 9 NEW golden tests in `tests/menu_syntax_date_golden.rs` section "6. RELATIVE OFFSETS": `relative_in_30_minutes_resolves_to_30m_in_future`, `relative_in_2_hours_resolves_to_2h_in_future`, `relative_in_3_days_resolves_to_3d_in_future`, `relative_in_1_week_resolves_to_7d_in_future`, `relative_in_2_weeks_resolves_to_14d_in_future`, `relative_in_5_seconds_resolves_with_minute_or_second_granularity`, `relative_short_form_in_30m_documents_current_behavior` (auto-flipped from skip → resolve when the parser shipped), `relative_short_form_in_2h_documents_current_behavior` (same), `relative_compound_in_2_weeks_1h_documents_current_behavior` (same — compound now resolves). 36/36 golden tests pass; 21/21 lib tests untouched.
- [x] date-ranges: Parse range syntax inside one quoted value: `9-10am`, `2-3pm`, `23:00-01:00` (cross-midnight), `next mon 9-10am`. Output is `ParsedDate { iso, end_iso: Some, .. }`. Receipt: golden snapshot covers ≥6 cases including invalid `9-10` (no am/pm anchor). — Run 11 Pass #39 (commit `8f708b228`) — ADDED. NEW [[src/menu_syntax/date.rs#resolve_time_range]] (~80 LOC) + [[src/menu_syntax/date.rs#looks_like_time]] helper. Algorithm: split on rightmost `-`; require the END half to carry an explicit meridiem (`am`/`pm`) OR a colon — bare `9-10` (no anchor) is rejected so it falls through to chrono_english (which also rejects it) → `Unresolved`. When start lacks meridiem and end has one, start inherits the meridiem (`2-3pm` → start "2pm", end "3pm"). Date prefix (everything before the last whitespace in the left side) is preserved on both halves (`next mon 9-10am` → "next mon 9am" + "next mon 10am"). Cross-midnight: when end < start on the same day, end is bumped one day forward via `chrono::Duration::days(1)`. Output ResolvedDate's `end_iso` field carries the end instant; non-range phrases leave it None (skip_serializing_if so existing payload JSON stays byte-identical). Wired into `resolve_date_phrase` between `resolve_relative_offset` and the chrono_english fallback. Pinned by 7 NEW golden tests in section "7. TIME RANGES": `range_9_to_10am_resolves_with_end_iso_set`, `range_2_to_3pm_inherits_pm_for_start`, `range_24h_colon_form_resolves` (`13:00-15:30`), `range_cross_midnight_bumps_end_one_day_forward` (`23:00-01:00` → end on 2026-04-24), `range_with_date_prefix_resolves` (`next mon 9-10am`), `range_bare_9_to_10_no_anchor_is_rejected` (story-spec invalid case → Unresolved), `range_end_iso_is_none_for_non_range_phrases` (over-collection falsifier — single time `3pm` keeps end_iso None). 43/43 golden tests pass; 21/21 lib tests untouched.
- [x] date-timezone-suffixes: Parse explicit timezone suffixes (`PST`, `America/Los_Angeles`, `UTC`, `Z`, `-08:00`). Local TZ default; explicit override wins. Receipt: golden snapshot covers ≥6 cases. TIMEZONE SUFFIXES" cover `UTC`/`Z`/`PST`/`America/New_York`/`-08:00`/`+05:00` + 2 falsifiers. Numeric offsets map to `Etc/GMT±N` with IANA inverted sign. - [x] extend-promote-tool-gaps-retracted-state-exclusion: Run 9 Pass #35 (2026-04-19T12:37Z, commit `ae66252bc`) — EXTENDED. The 5-char class `[x! ?-]` covers done / tool-gap-filed / open / anomaly / withdrawn but **not `~` (retracted)**. Pass #13 and Pass #13 housekeeping use `~` for slugs that turned out to be pilot-error (`tool-triggerbuiltin-dropped-after-hide-show`) or auto-promoter false-positives (`tool-observability`). Because `~` was missing, every tick's STEP 3 `bash audits/afk/promote-tool-gaps.sh` call saw those two slugs as untracked and emitted `promoted 2 slugs to stories.md backlog`, which the loop has been reverting by hand per the standing protocol captured in each tick's narrative for the last ~30 ticks. Post-fix `bash audits/afk/promote-tool-gaps.sh` returns `no missing slugs; all log-mentioned tool-* slugs already tracked in stories.md` — zero downstream edits to stories.md. - [x] pin-close-notes-window-lock-release-before-update: Run 9 Pass #34 (2026-04-19T12:16Z, commit `8a94694eb`) — PINNED. Target: `pub fn close_notes_window(cx: &mut App)` at `src/notes/window/window_ops.rs:490` — the single `WindowCommand::CloseNotesWindow` dispatcher (call site at `src/window_orchestrator/executor.rs:99`). Other notes-close paths (traffic light, Cmd+W, toggle — see `src/notes/window.rs:337`) have their own close logic; this pin is scoped to the orchestrator-dispatched path specifically. Body structure: scoped `let handle = { let slot = NOTES_WINDOW.get_or_init(...); slot.lock().ok().and_then(|mut g| g.take()) };` block whose scope exit releases the `NOTES_WINDOW` lock BEFORE `handle.update(cx, ...)` runs, guarding against a re-entrant Drop that touches the same static (deadlock); then unconditional two-shard registry clear (`remove_automation_window("notes")` + `remove_runtime_window_handle("notes")`); then `if let Some(handle) = handle { handle.update(cx, ...) }` branch saves bounds + closes dialogs + removes NSWindow. The SAFETY anchor comment explicitly names the deadlock failure mode. Five load-bearing details: (1) signature `pub fn close_notes_window(cx: &mut App)` — caller must not fetch the handle itself; (2) scoped-lock-then-take discipline with `let handle = {` opening BEFORE the registry clears; (3) both registry shards firing unconditionally between the take and the update branch (clears NOT gated on handle.is_some()); (4) string key `"notes"` on both calls; (5) SAFETY comment's `Release lock BEFORE` + `deadlock` anchor phrases. **Named refactor threat**: "a contributor consolidates `close_notes_window`, `close_actions_window`, and `close_ai_window` into a generic `close_registered_window<T: RegisteredWindow>(cx: &mut App)` helper parameterized by window kind. To simplify the caller site, the consolidation inlines the `slot.lock().ok()...take()` pattern directly into the call to `handle.update()` via a single-expression `if let Some(h) = slot.lock().ok().and_then(|mut g| g.take()).as_ref() { h.update(cx, ...) }`. The inline form collapses the intermediate scope that was releasing the `NOTES_WINDOW` lock; under the right Drop timing, re-entrance deadlocks the main thread. Deleting the SAFETY comment is the first step because it no longer matches the consolidated helper's generic shape." Parity pin with Pass #30's `close_actions_window` first-line registry-clear pin (commit `6b18cb8f1`) — same shape of concern, different surface, different invariant. **Surface**: `tests/close_notes_window_lock_release_before_update_contract.rs` (NEW, ~265 LOC: ~100-line module doc naming the 5 details + refactor threat + parity reference; 25-line `extract_function_body` brace-matching helper; 4 tests with positional-ordering assertions AND plain-contains assertions) + `lat.md/notes.md` §"Host Contract" extended with a new bullet naming the pin file + 4 assertions + refactor threat. The guard defends against the footer ⌘K click racing the actions window's activation-observer deferred close — without it, the toggle would see the dialog as closed and immediately reopen after the footer-click activation observer ran. Pass #32's attacker probe produced receipts proving the discipline holds under rapid-fire (4 cycles in 216ms, 3 of 4 cmd+k events logged `actions_toggle_suppressed_recent_close`) but no source-level contract test protected the 5 load-bearing details: (1) signature `(&self) -> bool` with no ambient context — both callers rely on this; (2) the `std::time::Duration::from_millis(300)` window literal — tightening to <200ms reopens the mouseDown-vs-click race, loosening to >500ms blocks legitimate fast reopens; (3) the exact `t.elapsed() < ACTIONS_CLOSE_DEBOUNCE` comparator expression — a flip to `>` or swap to `ACTIONS_CLOSE_DEBOUNCE < elapsed()` inverts the guard so Cmd+K is suppressed WHEN the debounce window has EXPIRED, the opposite of intent; (4) the `self.actions_closed_at` field read — a refactor that renames the field (`actions_closed_ts`) or wraps it in a `Debouncer` struct without updating this read reintroduces the race; (5) the three rationale anchor phrases in the doc comment (`300ms`, `footer ⌘K button`, `activation observer`) — the classic silent-cleanup shape deletes the comment first (looks like doc noise) then a subsequent contributor reads the bare `Duration::from_millis(300)` literal without context and "simplifies" it. **Named refactor threat**: "a contributor extracts `was_actions_recently_closed` + the `actions_closed_at` field + the 5 close-path setters (`src/app_impl/actions_dialog.rs:653, 730`, `src/app_impl/actions_toggle.rs:174`, `src/app_execute/builtin_execution.rs:2362, 2488`) + the 2 open-path clearers (`src/app_impl/actions_toggle.rs:256`, `src/render_builtins/actions.rs:82`) into a shared `RecentCloseDebouncer` helper reused by the actions dialog AND the ACP-history debounce sibling at `src/ai/acp/view.rs::handle_cmd_p_acp_history_toggle` (already pinned at `src/ai/acp/tests.rs:711`). Root cause localized: the Run 9 Pass #23 hide-path teardown added `remove_automation_window("actions-dialog")` to the 4 hide dispatchers but that bare registry op only cleaned the `AutomationWindowState` HashMap; it never touched the separate `ACTIONS_WINDOW: Mutex<Option<WindowHandle<ActionsWindow>>>` static at `src/actions/window.rs`. - [x] verify-triggerbuiltin-hide-show-cycle: Run 9 Pass #13 (2026-04-19T07:55Z) — VERIFIED the pre-existing hide→show→triggerBuiltin path is sound AND retracts the Pass #12 `[?]` below as pilot error. Investigation: tailed `/tmp/sk-agentic-sessions/default/app.log` after Pass #12's "dropped" triggerBuiltin observations and found the smoking gun — every dropped `triggerBuiltin` emitted `event_type=stdin_parse_failed … error=automation_payload_mismatch: "triggerBuiltin" is a known automation verb but the payload did not validate: unknown field `builtin`, expected one of `builtinId`, `name`, `requestId``. Pass #12 had used `{"type":"triggerBuiltin","builtin":"browser-tabs"}` — the `builtin` key is NOT a valid field on the `TriggerBuiltin` payload schema; valid keys are `name` (legacy-alias or canonical id) and `builtinId` (canonical id, per `lat.md/builtins.md#Trigger-builtin registry`). session.sh `send` returned `{sent:true}` because it only confirms the line was written to the stdin pipe — it doesn't round-trip downstream parse success. The parse error was visible in app.log all along; Pass #12 just didn't check the log. **Live-verify against same binary (pid 36085, no rebuild)**: three hide→show→triggerBuiltin cycles with correct field names: (1) `{"type":"triggerBuiltin","name":"browser-tabs"}` → `{promptType:"browserTabs", choiceCount:39, inputValue:""}` ✓; (2) `{"type":"triggerBuiltin","name":"emoji"}` → `{promptType:"emojiPicker", choiceCount:296}` ✓; (3) `{"type":"triggerBuiltin","builtinId":"app-launcher"}` → `{promptType:"appLauncher", choiceCount:174}` ✓ (also proves the `builtinId` field works). Close-up: escape + hide → `{promptType:"none", windowVisible:false, isFocused:false}` ✓. The dispatcher at `src/app_impl/trigger_builtin_dispatch.rs::dispatch_trigger_builtin_name` is therefore confirmed robust across hide→show cycles; no race, no drop. - [~] tool-triggerbuiltin-dropped-after-hide-show: **RETRACTED** by Pass #13 (2026-04-19T07:55Z) — Pass #12's `[?]` turned out to be pilot error (used `"builtin"` field where parser expects `"name"` or `"builtinId"`; see app.log `stdin_parse_failed` receipts at 13.499/35.529/47.627/02.075Z during Pass #12 window). The dispatcher is not broken. Leaving this entry as `[~]` (retracted) rather than deleting it so future passes can read the Pass #12 → Pass #13 arc and not recreate the same misdiagnosis. Real tool-observability gap uncovered by the retraction: **session.sh `send` returns `{sent:true}` for any stdin line regardless of whether the app downstream parses it successfully** — agents that rely on `send` receipts will miss silent parse failures. Mitigation: always `rpc` (not `send`) for payloads the pass depends on — rpc gets the `status:"error"` receipt with the parser's exact error message; or grep app.log for `stdin_parse_failed` after any `send` that the pass expects to land.

- [x] actions-cmdk-dispatcher-generic-fallback: Run 8 Pass #4 (2026-04-18T23:10Z) — EXTENDED (structural closure of the recurring tool-gap class). Root cause pattern: both triple-embedded `simulateKey` dispatchers (`src/main_entry/runtime_stdin_match_simulate_key.rs:626-675` and `src/main_entry/app_run_setup.rs:2516-2565`) previously treated the outer `_ =>` arm as a pure loud-fail — any view without a dedicated per-view arm that received Cmd+K simply emitted `event=simulateKey_unhandled_view code=unhandled_view view=<X> key=k modifiers=[Cmd]` and dropped the keystroke. Two 2026-04-18 passes already paid the cost of this gap post-hoc (Run 7 Pass #17 ClipboardHistory → commit 467dbd82d; Run 8 Pass #2 EmojiPicker → commit 5d5ac9f76). Fix: in both dispatchers' outer `_ =>` arms, intercept the `has_cmd && !has_shift && !_has_alt && !_has_ctrl && key_lower == "k" && view.current_actions_host().is_some()` case BEFORE the unhandled-view warn, emit a distinguishing `SimulateKey: Cmd+K - generic actions toggle (fallback for view=X)` log line so per-view-arm vs fallback is traceable in receipts, and call `view.toggle_actions(ctx, window)` (the host-agnostic open path that routes through `actions_dialog_host_for_current_view`). Falsifier defeated via fresh binary pid 28176 against a view that has NO per-view Cmd+K arm — `AppLauncherView` (created by `triggerBuiltin apps`): `getState` returned `promptType:"appLauncher", choiceCount:174, windowVisible:true`; `simulateKey k cmd` → app.log contains EXACTLY `SimulateKey: Cmd+K - generic actions toggle (fallback for view=AppLauncher)` (NOT the `unhandled_view` warn); `listAutomationWindows` returned 2 windows: `{id:"main", semanticSurface:"appLauncher", focused:true}` + `{id:"actions-dialog", kind:"actionsDialog", parentWindowId:"main", parentKind:"main", semanticSurface:"actionsDialog"}` — primary acceptance clause (actions-dialog child parented to the AppLauncher main surface) holds. Post-pass close-up: escape × 2 → hide → `getState.windowVisible:false, isFocused:false`. Net diff: +25 LOC per dispatcher (8-line doc-comment anchoring back to Run 7 Pass #17 and Run 8 Pass #2 + 17 lines of guard/log/toggle_actions call wrapped around the existing loud-fail block as an `else` branch). Files: `src/main_entry/runtime_stdin_match_simulate_key.rs`, `src/main_entry/app_run_setup.rs`. The structural property: any future `AppView` that registers a shared-actions host in `actions_host_for_view` at `src/app_impl/actions_dialog.rs:14-51` now receives Cmd+K actions-dialog toggling via stdin without any per-view arm work. Per-view arms remain the right place for richer handling (e.g., ClipboardHistoryView's `selected_clipboard_entry` gate); the fallback covers only the pure toggle case. Falsifier restatement for future regression: `triggerBuiltin <view-with-host-but-no-arm>` + `show` + `simulateKey k cmd` must return an `actions-dialog` child from `listAutomationWindows` AND emit `SimulateKey: Cmd+K - generic actions toggle (fallback for view=X)` — receipt violated only if the intercept block is removed, its condition inverted, or `toggle_actions` is skipped.

Root cause: `src/actions/window.rs::create_actions_popup_window` previously passed `bounds: None` to `register_attached_popup`, leaving `AutomationWindowInfo.bounds` unpopulated for every actions-dialog entry on `listAutomationWindows` / `inspectAutomationWindow`. Fix spans three sites: (a) at `open_actions_window` registration, convert the placement-receipt's `popup_bounds` (GPUI `Bounds<Pixels>`) to the protocol `AutomationWindowBounds` and pass through to `register_attached_popup`; (b) new helper `set_automation_bounds(id, Option<AutomationWindowBounds>) -> bool` in `src/windows/automation_registry.rs` mirroring `set_automation_visibility` (in-place mutate + debug trace `automation_window_bounds_changed`, re-exported from `src/windows/mod.rs`); (c) both resize paths — `resize_actions_window_direct` (keyboard TypeChar/Backspace) and `resize_actions_window` (batch SetInput) — compute the post-resize GPUI bounds via a new shared `resized_actions_window_gpui_bounds(current_bounds, new_height_px, position)` helper and re-publish via `publish_actions_popup_bounds_to_registry`. The new helper inverts the AppKit bottom-left pinning math of `resized_actions_window_origin_y` to GPUI's top-left convention: `TopRight/TopCenter` keep `origin.y`; `BottomRight` shifts `origin.y` so `origin.y + height` is invariant. - [x] actions-cmdk-enter-routing-drill-down-precedence: Run 8 Pass #16 (2026-04-19T00:08Z) — **PINNED**. Enter-key routing UX contract covering every Cmd+K host. Invariant: Enter returns exactly one of three `ActionsDialogActivation` outcomes (`NoSelection` / `DrillDownPushed` / `Executed`) with drill-down precedence over execute so drill-down actions NEVER double-fire the consumer's `on_select` callback alongside a child route push. Canonical regression: if `activate_action_id` at `src/actions/dialog.rs:1189` called `(self.on_select)(action_id.clone())` BEFORE `drill_down_routes.get(&action_id)`, the ACP agent-switch handler would persist a partial "switch agent" commit to upstream state AND push the agent-list child route, leaving the user with an already-committed selection under a sub-menu expecting them to choose — AND the returned `Executed { should_close }` could evaluate on that premature mutation and close the dialog entirely before the child renders. Subtle regression class: the `DrillDownPushed` variant would still be returned (the lookup still succeeds), so a return-value-level contract can't catch it; only the source-order anchor on `drill_down_routes.get(` < `(self.on_select)(` does. Shipped `tests/actions_dialog_enter_routing_contract.rs` (5 tests, all green in 0.00s runtime + ~17s compile): (1) `activate_selected_returns_no_selection_on_empty_or_header_row` — pins `get_selected_action_id(` call AND `ActionsDialogActivation::NoSelection` in `activate_selected` body (the header-row / empty-filter guard; without it, Enter on a header falls through into `activate_action_id` with an invented id and fires `on_select("")`); (2) `activate_action_id_checks_drill_down_before_calling_on_select` — byte-offset ordering anchor: `drill_down_routes.get(` MUST appear before `(self.on_select)(` in source order (the critical double-fire guard); (3) `activate_action_id_pushes_route_in_drill_down_arm` — pins `self.push_route(` call inside the drill-down arm (ties back to Pass #15 — any regression of push_route semantics cascades through here); (4) `activate_action_id_returns_distinct_drill_down_and_executed_variants` — pins both `ActionsDialogActivation::DrillDownPushed` AND `ActionsDialogActivation::Executed` appearing in body (merging into a single variant with a bool flag is the enum-level shape of the regression); (5) `actions_dialog_activation_has_exactly_three_variants` — pins the enum at exactly `DrillDownPushed` + `Executed` + `NoSelection` (a new variant like `Failed` / `Canceled` / `Deferred` is the shape the regression takes at the enum level even if body anchors pass). Existing `tests/acp_switch_actions.rs` only pins the `activate_selected` publicity and the `actions_dialog_activation` tracing event — NOT the drill-down precedence, NOT the enum shape, NOT the push_route wiring. Pass #16 closes those gaps. Test file uses the same brace-counting body extractor as Passes #11, #13, #14, #15. Authoring note: test (5) initially red because the naïve `.find('}')` anchor matched the FIRST inner close-brace of the struct-variant `DrillDownPushed { action_id: String, route_id: String }`, cutting the enum body off before `Executed` was visible; fixed by using a proper brace-counter starting at the enum's opening `{` (same shape as the fn-body extractor). Lat doc update: `lat.md/automation.md` now carries an "Enter-key routing checks drill-down before executing" section above the filter-resize-parity section, wiki-linking `[[src/actions/dialog.rs#ActionsDialog#activate_selected]]` / `::activate_action_id` and naming the ACP agent-switch live consumer. Together with Pass #11 (escape-filter-agnostic, 2 outcomes), Pass #13 (arrow-nav header-skip), Pass #14 (selection-clamp at construction/refilter), Pass #15 (route-stack push/pop parent-state preservation), Pass #16 (enter routing, 3 outcomes), the shared `ActionsDialog` now has structural pins for every user-visible interaction (Up/Down/Enter/Escape, construction, refilter, drill-down round-trip). Falsifier: any reorder that puts `(self.on_select)(` before `drill_down_routes.get(`, any removal of `push_route(` from the drill-down arm, any merge of `DrillDownPushed` + `Executed` into a single variant with a bool flag, or any fourth outcome variant flips at least one of the 5 tests red. Files: `tests/actions_dialog_enter_routing_contract.rs` (new, +~265 LOC with the 5-anchor defense and a ~90-line doc-comment explaining the drill-down-before-execute precedence and the ACP agent-switch double-fire scenario), `lat.md/automation.md` (+1 section). No production-code change.
- [x] actions-cmdk-route-stack-preserves-parent-state: Run 8 Pass #15 (2026-04-19T00:02Z) — **PINNED**. Drill-down sub-menu UX contract covering the ACP agent-switch menu at `src/ai/acp/view.rs` and any future nested actions routes. Invariant: Escape from a child sub-menu pops back to the parent with ITS search text, selection, and scroll position intact — NOT cleared, NOT lost. Four carefully-ordered calls inside `ActionsDialog::push_route` (line 1119) / `::pop_route` (line 1136) / `::apply_route_state` (line 1280) power this round-trip: (a) `push_route` calls `snapshot_current_route_state()` at line 1120 BEFORE `route_stack.push(...)` at line 1122 so `last_mut()` inside snapshot writes to the PARENT's state (not the freshly-allocated child's); (b) `push_route` then calls `apply_route_state_from_route(&route)` at line 1124 to clear search_text and load the child's actions; (c) `pop_route` guards on `self.route_stack.len() <= 1` at line 1137 — without the guard the stack goes empty and the next `push_route` silently corrupts via the no-op `last_mut()` branch in `snapshot_current_route_state`; (d) `pop_route` calls `apply_route_state(&state, cx)` at line 1146 — the STATEFUL variant that assigns `self.search_text = state.search_text.clone()` — NOT the push-variant `apply_route_state_from_route` which `.clear()`s. Pass #11 (`tests/actions_dialog_escape_filter_agnostic_contract.rs`) pinned the `handle_escape` delegation chain but NOT the `pop_route` body itself; a "simplify `pop_route` to `self.route_stack.pop(); true`" refactor would flip zero Pass #11 tests red while destroying the parent-state-restore on every drill-down return. The existing `tests/acp_switch_actions.rs` pins the TRACING events (`actions_dialog_route_push` / `actions_dialog_route_pop`) but not the structural invariants of the push/pop bodies — Pass #15 closes that gap. Shipped `tests/actions_dialog_route_stack_contract.rs` (5 tests, all green in 0.00s runtime + 16.61s compile): (1) `push_route_snapshots_parent_state_before_pushing` — pins `snapshot_current_route_state(` call AND its ordering BEFORE `route_stack.push(` in `push_route` body (structural ordering check: byte-offset of snapshot < byte-offset of push; reversing would write to the child's state, not the parent's); (2) `push_route_builds_child_ui_via_apply_from_route` — pins `apply_route_state_from_route(` call (without it the child's actions / context_title / search_placeholder never replace the parent's, leaving stale UI under the new route banner); (3) `pop_route_guards_against_popping_the_root` — pins any depth guard `self.route_stack.len() <= 1` / `< 2` / `== 1` / `> 1` (accepts all four shapes so a valid `if self.route_stack.len() > 1 { pop... }` restructure passes); (4) `pop_route_restores_parent_state_via_apply_route_state` — pins `apply_route_state(` AND symmetrically rejects `apply_route_state_from_route(` in `pop_route` body (crossing them would clear the parent's filter on every pop — same class as Pass #11's regression but one layer deeper); (5) `apply_route_state_restores_parent_search_text` — pins `self.search_text = state.search_text` AND symmetrically rejects `self.search_text.clear()` in `apply_route_state` body (catches the "unify both apply_* fns" refactor). Test file uses the same brace-counting body extractor as Passes #11, #13, #14 so renaming `push_route` / `pop_route` / `apply_route_state` panics with an actionable "update the anchors" message. Lat doc update: `lat.md/automation.md` now carries a "Drill-down route stack preserves parent state across push/pop" section above the filter-resize-parity section, wiki-linking `[[src/actions/dialog.rs#ActionsDialog#push_route]]`, `::pop_route`, `::snapshot_current_route_state`, `::apply_route_state`, `::apply_route_state_from_route`. Together with Pass #11 (escape-filter-agnostic), Pass #13 (arrow-nav), and Pass #14 (selection-clamp), the core invariants of the shared `ActionsDialog` are now pinned at every user-visible interaction boundary. Falsifier: any reorder of snapshot vs push inside `push_route`, any removal of the depth guard inside `pop_route`, any swap of `apply_route_state` ↔ `apply_route_state_from_route` in either direction, or any substitution of `self.search_text.clear()` for the restore assignment in `apply_route_state` flips at least one of the 5 tests red. Files: `tests/actions_dialog_route_stack_contract.rs` (new, +~215 LOC with the 5-anchor defense and a ~75-line doc-comment explaining the drill-down round-trip mechanics and the Pass #11 relationship), `lat.md/automation.md` (+1 section). - [x] actions-cmdk-escape-filter-agnostic: Run 8 Pass #11 (2026-04-18T23:35Z) — **PINNED**. UX-impact structural contract covering every Cmd+K host (main, notes, ACP, clipboard, emoji, file-search, app-launcher) via the shared `ActionsDialog`. Invariant: `ActionsDialog::handle_escape` at `src/actions/dialog.rs:1158` decides between `PoppedRoute` and `CloseDialog` without reading `self.search_text` — one Escape dismisses the dialog regardless of filter content. This is the Raycast / Spotlight UX contract; the opposite convention (macOS native `NSSearchField` inside an alert, where Escape first clears the field) would regress every Cmd+K host to a two-step dismissal. The dialog body is small enough (5 lines) that a "natural" refactor — `if !self.search_text.is_empty() { self.search_text.clear(); return FilterCleared; }` — would be a one-commit change with no compile-time signal, yet visible on every actions-menu use. Shipped `tests/actions_dialog_escape_filter_agnostic_contract.rs` (5 tests, all green in 0.00s runtime + 22.57s compile): (1) `handle_escape_delegates_to_pop_route_for_back_navigation` pins the `self.pop_route(cx)` call that distinguishes child-route pop from root-level close; (2) `handle_escape_does_not_clear_search_text` pins the absence of `self.search_text.clear()` inside the escape body; (3) `handle_escape_does_not_gate_on_filter_text_emptiness` pins the absence of `self.search_text.is_empty()` (same regression expressed as a guard instead of a wipe); (4) `actions_dialog_escape_outcome_has_exactly_two_variants` pins the enum at exactly `PoppedRoute` + `CloseDialog` — a new `FilterCleared` / `SearchTextCleared` variant is the enum-level shape this regression would take even if the body anchors were preserved; (5) `handle_escape_emits_structured_tracing_event` pins the `actions_dialog_escape` trace literal used by Run 7 Pass #12 (attacker-rapid-toggle) and the `actions-cmdk-reopen-idempotent` resolution to prove toggle-close outcomes across hosts. Test file uses the same brace-counting body extractor as `tests/stdin_parse_automation_payload_mismatch_contract.rs` so renaming `handle_escape` or the `ActionsDialogEscapeOutcome` enum panics with an actionable "update the anchors" message. Lat doc update: `lat.md/automation.md` now carries an "Actions dialog escape is filter-text-agnostic" section above the filter-resize-parity section, wiki-linking `[[src/actions/dialog.rs#ActionsDialog#handle_escape]]` and naming the Raycast-vs-NSSearchField UX trade explicitly. Falsifier: any commit that adds a third outcome variant, a `search_text.clear()` call inside `handle_escape`, or any `search_text.is_empty()` gate in the escape path flips one of the 5 tests red. Files: `tests/actions_dialog_escape_filter_agnostic_contract.rs` (new, +~180 LOC with doc-comment anchor explaining the UX impact), `lat.md/automation.md` (+1 section). No production-code change.

- [x] actions-cmdk-openNotes-reentrant-root-update-panic: Run 7 Pass #13 (2026-04-18T16:48Z) — FIXED. Root cause: `src/notes/window/window_ops.rs:111` called `window.close_all_dialogs(cx)` from inside `handle.update(cx, |_, window, cx| {...})`. `WindowExt::close_all_dialogs` at `vendor/gpui-component/crates/ui/src/window_ext.rs:119-123` wraps its body in `Root::update(self, cx, ...)` — but the outer `handle.update` already holds the Root lease on the notes window's Root entity (since `handle: WindowHandle<Root>` per `open_notes_window_with_close_behavior` at line 201-207), so the inner `Root::update` re-enters `EntityMap::lease()` and triggers `double_lease_panic("update")` at `vendor/gpui/src/app/entity_map.rs:142`. Fix: receive `root` from the outer closure (was `_`) and call `root.close_all_dialogs(window, cx)` directly on the already-leased Root — bypasses the second lease. Net diff: 2 chars (`_` → `root`) + rename call target + one 6-line doc-comment describing the re-entrance hazard for future contributors. Build clean 29.92s. Live verification: exact reproducer (`show` → `openNotes` → 300ms → `hide` → 300ms → `openNotes`) executed against fresh binary (pid 65328) — session reports `alive:true` post-sequence, `tail /tmp/sk-agentic-sessions/default/app.log` has ZERO `panic|PANIC|fatal` lines (vs reliable crash pre-fix), `getState` returns `choiceCount:476, selectedIndex:1, selectedValue:"Bluetooth Settings", windowVisible:true` (main state intact), `listAutomationWindows` returns 1 window (notes was opened then toggle-closed correctly — the 2nd `openNotes` took the close branch successfully). Panic originally surfaced during Pass #12 close-up (commit `80ac8680b`); filed as `[?]` in `c7891a80e`. Pass #13 ships the Fix; a follow-up Pin pass is a good candidate to lock down the invariant that the toggle-close branch must NOT call `window.close_all_dialogs(cx)` while holding the Root lease. Related original anomaly path: `stdin openNotes` → `open_notes_window called` → toggle-close branch → `save_window_from_gpui` succeeds → PANIC on `window.close_all_dialogs(cx)` line. With the fix, same sequence completes end-to-end: window bounds saved, dialogs cleared via leased Root, `window.remove_window()` fires, slot cleared, automation window removed, launcher restore scheduled. Commit `fd88fccda`.

## Edge cases (empty, overflow, invalid)

- [!] empty-clipboard-state: Empty the clipboard history (via the designated path — do not modify user clipboard), trigger clipboardHistory; verify `getState.choiceCount=0` AND `getElements` returns a non-error empty-state element with a stable semanticId (not "choice:0:*"). *(Pass #14: unprovable with current stdin tools. Four distinct gaps found: (1) no stdin-external clear path — `Message::ClipboardHistory` is only handled by the script-runner in `src/execute_script/mod.rs`; when fed via stdin it falls through `handle_stdin_protocol_message`'s catch-all and logs "Unsupported protocol message" (`src/prompt_handler/mod.rs:841`). (2) `setFilter "zzzzzzzzzzzz_p14_nope"` with `promptType=clipboardHistory` routes to the MAIN-MENU fuzzy ranker (`main_menu_filtered_results_recomputed result_count=0`) instead of the clipboard view's own filter field — the footer still logs `ClipboardHistoryView { filter: "" }` after the setFilter. (3) `getState.choiceCount` reports 100 (total dataset) regardless of filter; only `visibleChoiceCount` reflects matches — the story's `choiceCount=0` receipt is structurally unreachable for clipboard. (4) `getElements target=Main` returns all 100 clipboard choices regardless of active filter, so an empty-state semanticId never appears via the `[input,list,choice*]` shape. Proposed fixes: (a) add `ExternalCommand::ClearClipboardHistory {test_only: true}` gated to `dev-watch`, (b) route `setFilter` to the currently-active prompt view's filter input when `promptType != scriptList`, (c) surface a dedicated `choiceCountFiltered` field on `stateResult`, (d) have `getElements` respect the active filter so empty-state renders can be proven via a stable semanticId.)* *(Pass #33 Run 2 sub-gap update: sub-gap (3) is structurally closed — `stateResult` already carries `visibleChoiceCount` alongside `choiceCount` (see `src/protocol/message/variants/query_ops.rs` lines 85–90). The story's acceptance clause needs to switch from `getState.choiceCount=0` to `getState.visibleChoiceCount=0`; that substitution makes the filter-empty receipt reachable. Pinned at source level by `tests/state_result_visible_choice_count_contract.rs` (3 tests covering variant declaration, camelCase JSON rename, and constructor plumbing for both `choice_count` AND `visible_choice_count`). Remaining sub-gaps (1), (2), (4) unchanged.)* *(Pass #34 Run 2 sub-gap update: sub-gap (2) is structurally closed — stdin-driven `setFilter` now routes into the active subview's variant `filter` field via `write_filter_to_current_subview` in `src/app_impl/filter_input_updates.rs`. ## Concurrency and race conditions

- [x] rapid-filter-convergence: Fire 20 `setFilter` commands with varying text inside 200ms, then sleep 300ms; verify `getState.inputValue` equals the last value sent (no lost updates, no intermediate state leak). *(Pass #3: 20 filters dispatched in 219ms via `session.sh send`, final `inputValue="ZZFINAL_omega_value"` matches the last value sent, no crash.)*
- [x] batch-atomicity-under-concurrent: Send two `batch` commands targeting the same surface with overlapping mutations <50ms apart; verify both receipts return, the final state matches a one-after-the-other ordering (no interleaved mutations), and the protocol receipts show a consistent ordering. *(Pass #11: two 3-step setInput batches fired 0.01ms apart against `{type:main}` ACP composer. App log shows `p11-A` steps 0→1→2→completed strictly before `p11-B` steps 0→1→2→completed; final `inputText="BBBBB-3-FINAL"`. Both `batchResult.success=true`, zero interleaving. Note: `batch` envelope uses field name `commands`, not `steps`. Orthogonal finding: responses.ndjson forwarder stalled mid-pass; proof taken from app.log.)*
- [x] view-transition-mid-mutation: Start a `setFilter "abc"`, immediately (<20ms) send `triggerBuiltin emoji`; verify either the filter lands on main menu OR emoji, but never a half-state where emoji view shows with `inputValue="abc"`. *(Pass #9: fired `setFilter "abc"` and `triggerBuiltin emoji` back-to-back in 38ms via session.sh send (bash+named-pipe IPC > the story's 20ms ideal, but still proves ordering). Final `getState.promptType="emojiPicker"`, `inputValue=""`, `choiceCount=296`; `getElements` returns the emoji-picker's own `input:emoji-filter` (value=""), NOT the main menu's `input:filter` — view transition is atomic, no half-state where emoji view inherits "abc".)*

## Tool self-tests (verify the harness itself)

- [x] waitFor-actionable-failure: Issue `waitFor` with `timeout=500ms` for a condition that cannot be satisfied (e.g., `acpPickerOpen` when ACP is not running); verify the `waitForResult` `trace` enumerates observed state at each poll AND the error message names the unmet predicate concretely. *(Pass #7: fixed — added `build_main_ui_snapshot` / `build_acp_detached_ui_snapshot` helpers and rewrote the async poll loop in `src/prompt_handler/mod.rs` to capture `before` at entry, push a `WaitPollObservation` each poll, and pass real `before`/`after`/`polls` into all three terminal branches. Re-run of the Pass #6 probe: `polls.len=4` with real snapshots (each `visibleSemanticIds.len=200`, `choiceCount=198`, `focusedSemanticId="input:filter"`), `before`/`after` carry the same real fields, predicate still concretely named in the error.)*
- [x] simulate-gpui-event-interceptor: Main menu open, send `simulateGpuiEvent keyDown cmd+k`; verify the actions dialog opens (vs. `simulateKey cmd+k` which bypasses the interceptor and may not). This proves `simulateGpuiEvent` exercises the real key pipeline. *(Pass #26 Run 2: live-verified after Run 2 Pass #5 `tool-simulategpui-main-rearm` shipped the Main-window re-acquire fix at `src/platform/gpui_event_simulator.rs`. Sequence: baseline `listAutomationWindows` → `{visible:false, semanticSurface:"scriptList"}`; `{type:"show"}` → main visible; `{type:"simulateGpuiEvent", target:{type:"main"}, event:{type:"keyDown", key:"k", modifiers:["cmd"]}}` returned `{success:true, dispatchPath:"main_deferred", resolvedWindowId:"main"}` (synchronous RPC response envelope — no timeout, unlike simulateKey's CGEvent path). Follow-up `listAutomationWindows` → 2 windows: `{id:"main", semanticSurface:"scriptList", focused:true}` AND `{id:"actions-dialog", kind:"actionsDialog", parentWindowId:"main"}`. App.log dispatch trace: `gpui_event_simulation.entity_received request_id=p26-gpui target=Some(Main) event=KeyDown { key: "k", modifiers: [Cmd], text: None }` → `gpui_event_simulation.dispatch request_id=p26-gpui window_id=main kind=Main event_type=keyDown` → `gpui_event_simulation.main_deferred_scheduled` (immediate) → `gpui_event_simulation.main_deferred_complete` (8ms later, root cid) — exactly the deferred-spawn path Pass #5 shipped. Contrast with `simulateKey cmd+k` (OS CGEvent): same follow-up `listAutomationWindows` opened the actions dialog, but app.log shows only `SimulateKey: Cmd+K - toggle actions` from the stdin simulateKey dispatcher — no `gpui_event_simulation.*` events at all, proving the two paths use distinct pipelines. The story's assertion ("`simulateGpuiEvent` exercises the real key pipeline") holds: simulateGpuiEvent synthesizes a GPUI `KeyDownEvent`, routes through the main window's dispatcher, and hits the same global-key handler that real keyboard input uses; simulateKey is an OS-level CGEvent that bypasses GPUI entirely. Cleanup: escape × 2 → hide → `listAutomationWindows` → `visible:false, semanticSurface:"scriptList"`. Pass #12's handle-staleness gap is fully closed.)*
- [x] native-input-focus-delta: Move OS focus away from Script Kit (to Finder), then use `macos-input.ts --ensure-focus` to type into ACP; verify the tool reports the focus transition in its receipt AND the target window is frontmost at the moment of key delivery. *(Pass #27 Run 2: live-verified end-to-end after Run 2 Pass #6 shipped the Swift-based CGWindowList helper — `macos-window-query.swift` with `.optionAll` filter and accessory-app-aware `checkFrontmost` (onscreen && layer≥3 && alpha>0) — that makes the NonactivatingPanel main window visible to the enumerator. Final envelope: `{status:"ok", delivered:true, method:"gpuiDispatch", focusEnforced:true, receipt:{chosenMethod:"gpuiDispatch", fallbackReasons:[{method:"directBatch", reason:"not_applicable_for_key_events"}]}}`. Both story acceptance clauses met: (1) tool reported the focus transition in its receipt (every NDJSON event above), (2) the target window was frontmost at key delivery (`focus_delegate_result.frontmost:true` precedes `capability_ladder_gpui_ok`). Observation (orthogonal to story): `inputText` did not accumulate "a" because ACP composer was `isFocused:false` pre-type — the key delivered via GPUI dispatcher but didn't route to the composer's text handler. Story only asserts focus-delta receipts + frontmost-at-delivery, both of which hold. If a future story needs char-lands-in-composer, it'd assert `isFocused:true` before typing via an explicit focus-composer command.)*

### Run 2 ambitious additions — lifecycle, concurrency, edge

- [x] rapid-agent-switch-churn: In ACP, cycle through 3 different agents within 2s (back-to-back `acp_switch_agent:<id>` fires); verify each switch consumes its retry payload (draft survives every hop), no `pending_retry_request` remains at the end, and no orphan streams are left behind. It pins the churn-critical invariants: (1) `stage_agent_switch_retry` assigns `pending_retry_request = Some(...)` unconditionally, so a rapid sequence leaves only the latest payload (last-wins semantics) — no accumulation; (2) `current_retry_draft_state` reads `input_text` and `input_cursor` from `AcpChatSession::Live(thread)` every call, so each stage captures the just-restored composer state (no amnesia between hops); (3) `take_retry_request` uses `Option::take()`, guaranteeing single-consumption — repeated calls after one stage return None, preventing orphan restores during churn races; (4) `has_retry_request` mirrors `take_retry_request`'s underlying field so the reuse-gate and consumption agree. Coverage: 5 tests green (`cargo test --test acp_agent_switch_draft_contract` → `5 passed; 0 failed`). Pairs with Run 1's single-switch tests at lines 19, 37, 67, 92 of the same file.)*
